/*
 * Stub CryptoKit framework for macOS 10.9 compatibility.
 * Exports the Swift-mangled symbols that the .NET runtime host links against.
 * These are never actually called by Celeste64 at runtime - they exist only
 * so dyld can resolve the symbols and load the binary.
 */

#include <stdlib.h>

/* For data symbols (type metadata, descriptors, etc.) we provide a block of zeroed memory */
static char _stub_data[4096] __attribute__((aligned(16)));

#define STUB_FUNC(name) \
    void name(void) { abort(); }

#define STUB_DATA(name) \
    void *name __attribute__((visibility("default"))) = (void*)_stub_data;

/* ChaChaPoly */
STUB_FUNC(_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO4open_5using14authenticating10Foundation4DataVAC9SealedBoxV_AA12SymmetricKeyVxtKAG0I8ProtocolRzlFZ)

STUB_FUNC(_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO5NonceV4dataAEx_tKc10Foundation12DataProtocolRzlufC)
STUB_FUNC(_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO5NonceVMa)
STUB_DATA(_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO5NonceVMn)
STUB_FUNC(_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO9SealedBoxV10ciphertext10Foundation4DataVvg)
STUB_FUNC(_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO9SealedBoxV3tag10Foundation4DataVvg)
STUB_FUNC(_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO9SealedBoxV5nonce10ciphertext3tagAeC5NonceV_xq_tKc10Foundation12DataProtocolRzAkLR_r0_lufC)

/* CryptoKitError */
STUB_DATA(_$s9CryptoKit0aB5ErrorO21authenticationFailureyA2CmFWC)
STUB_FUNC(_$s9CryptoKit0aB5ErrorOMa)

/* SymmetricKey */
STUB_FUNC(_$s9CryptoKit12SymmetricKeyV4dataACx_tc10Foundation15ContiguousBytesRzlufC)

📝 Write run_celeste64.sh


/Users/Jonathan/Downloads/Celeste64-v1.1.0-macOS-x64/run_celeste64.sh


#!/bin/bash
# Celeste64 launcher for macOS 10.9 compatibility
# Redirects missing framework/library loads to local stubs

DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "$0")" && pwd)"

export DYLD_FRAMEWORK_PATH="$DIR/compat:${DYLD_FRAMEWORK_PATH}"
export DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH="$DIR/compat/swift:${DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH}"

exec "$DIR/Celeste64" "$@"

📝 Write stub_system.c


/Users/Jonathan/Downloads/Celeste64-v1.1.0-macOS-x64/compat/stub_system.c


/*
 * System compatibility shim for macOS 10.9.
 * Provides stub implementations of functions added in macOS 10.10+
 * that the .NET 8 runtime references but Celeste64 doesn't actually use.
 */

#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <Security/Security.h>

/* ============================================================
 * CommonCrypto - CCRandomGenerateBytes (added 10.10)
 * ============================================================ */
int CCRandomGenerateBytes(void *bytes, size_t count) {
    /* Use /dev/urandom as fallback */
    int fd = open("/dev/urandom", O_RDONLY);
    if (fd < 0) return -1;
    ssize_t r = read(fd, bytes, count);
    close(fd);
    return (r == (ssize_t)count) ? 0 : -1;
}

/* ============================================================
 * Security framework - SecKey functions (added 10.12+)
 * ============================================================ */

/* errSecUnimplemented = -4 */
#define STUB_UNIMPLEMENTED (-4)

CFDataRef SecKeyCopyExternalRepresentation(SecKeyRef key, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

SecKeyRef SecKeyCreateWithData(CFDataRef keyData, CFDictionaryRef attributes, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)keyData; (void)attributes;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

SecKeyRef SecKeyCreateRandomKey(CFDictionaryRef parameters, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)parameters;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

CFDataRef SecKeyCreateSignature(SecKeyRef key, SecPadding algorithm,
                                CFDataRef dataToSign, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key; (void)algorithm; (void)dataToSign;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

Boolean SecKeyVerifySignature(SecKeyRef key, SecPadding algorithm,
                              CFDataRef signedData, CFDataRef signature,
                              CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key; (void)algorithm; (void)signedData; (void)signature;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return false;
}

CFDataRef SecKeyCreateEncryptedData(SecKeyRef key, SecPadding algorithm,
                                    CFDataRef plaintext, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key; (void)algorithm; (void)plaintext;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

CFDataRef SecKeyCreateDecryptedData(SecKeyRef key, SecPadding algorithm,
                                    CFDataRef ciphertext, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key; (void)algorithm; (void)ciphertext;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

SecKeyRef SecKeyCopyPublicKey(SecKeyRef key) {
    (void)key;
    return NULL;
}

CFDictionaryRef SecKeyCopyAttributes(SecKeyRef key) {
    (void)key;
    return NULL;
}

CFDataRef SecKeyCopyKeyExchangeResult(SecKeyRef publicKey, void *algorithm,
                                      SecKeyRef parameters, CFDictionaryRef requestedSize,
                                      CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)publicKey; (void)algorithm; (void)parameters; (void)requestedSize;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

/* SecCertificateCopyKey - added 10.14 */
SecKeyRef SecCertificateCopyKey(SecCertificateRef certificate) {
    (void)certificate;
    return NULL;
}

/* ============================================================
 * SSL/TLS ALPN functions (added 10.13.4)
 * ============================================================ */

OSStatus SSLCopyALPNProtocols(void *context, CFArrayRef *protocols) {
    (void)context;
    if (protocols) *protocols = NULL;
    return errSecUnimplemented;
}

OSStatus SSLSetALPNProtocols(void *context, CFArrayRef protocols) {
    (void)context; (void)protocols;
    return errSecUnimplemented;
}

📝 Write run_celeste64.sh


/Users/Jonathan/Downloads/Celeste64-v1.1.0-macOS-x64/run_celeste64.sh


#!/bin/bash
# Celeste64 launcher for macOS 10.9 compatibility
# Uses stub libraries for missing frameworks and system symbols

DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "$0")" && pwd)"

# Redirect missing framework/library loads to local stubs
export DYLD_FRAMEWORK_PATH="$DIR/compat:${DYLD_FRAMEWORK_PATH}"
export DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH="$DIR/compat/swift:${DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH}"

# Force flat namespace so our shim can provide missing system symbols
export DYLD_FORCE_FLAT_NAMESPACE=1

# Insert our compat shim for missing Security/CommonCrypto symbols
export DYLD_INSERT_LIBRARIES="$DIR/compat/libcompat.dylib"

exec "$DIR/Celeste64" "$@"

#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <sys/time.h>
#include <mach/mach_time.h>
#include <Security/Security.h>

/* ============================================================
 * POSIX - clock_gettime / clock_gettime_nsec_np (added 10.12)
 * ============================================================ */

#ifndef CLOCK_REALTIME
#define CLOCK_REALTIME  0
#define CLOCK_MONOTONIC 6
#define CLOCK_MONOTONIC_RAW 4
#define CLOCK_PROCESS_CPUTIME_ID 12
#define CLOCK_THREAD_CPUTIME_ID 16
#endif

struct compat_timespec {
    long tv_sec;
    long tv_nsec;
};

int clock_gettime(int clk_id, struct compat_timespec *tp) {
    if (clk_id == CLOCK_REALTIME) {
        struct timeval tv;
        gettimeofday(&tv, NULL);
        tp->tv_sec = tv.tv_sec;
        tp->tv_nsec = tv.tv_usec * 1000;
        return 0;
    } else {
        /* CLOCK_MONOTONIC and others - use mach_absolute_time */
        static mach_timebase_info_data_t timebase = {0, 0};
        if (timebase.denom == 0) mach_timebase_info(&timebase);
        uint64_t nsec = mach_absolute_time() * timebase.numer / timebase.denom;
        tp->tv_sec = (long)(nsec / 1000000000ULL);
        tp->tv_nsec = (long)(nsec % 1000000000ULL);
        return 0;
    }
}

uint64_t clock_gettime_nsec_np(int clk_id) {
    struct compat_timespec ts;
    clock_gettime(clk_id, &ts);
    return (uint64_t)ts.tv_sec * 1000000000ULL + (uint64_t)ts.tv_nsec;
}

/* ============================================================
 * POSIX *at() functions and time functions (added 10.10+)
 * ============================================================ */

#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <sys/param.h>
#include <errno.h>

/* fstatat - added 10.10 */
int fstatat_inode64(int fd, const char *path, struct stat *buf, int flag)
    __asm("_fstatat$INODE64");
int fstatat_inode64(int fd, const char *path, struct stat *buf, int flag) {
    /* If fd is AT_FDCWD or path is absolute, just use lstat/stat */
    if (path[0] == '/' || fd == -2 /*AT_FDCWD*/) {
        if (flag & 0x0020 /*AT_SYMLINK_NOFOLLOW*/)
            return lstat(path, buf);
        else
            return stat(path, buf);
    }
    /* For relative fd paths, construct full path via fcntl */
    char fdpath[MAXPATHLEN];
    if (fcntl(fd, F_GETPATH, fdpath) == -1) {
        errno = EBADF;
        return -1;
    }
    char fullpath[MAXPATHLEN];
    snprintf(fullpath, sizeof(fullpath), "%s/%s", fdpath, path);
    if (flag & 0x0020)
        return lstat(fullpath, buf);
    else
        return stat(fullpath, buf);
}

/* futimens - added 10.13 */
int futimens(int fd, const struct timespec times[2]) {
    struct timeval tv[2];
    if (times) {
        tv[0].tv_sec = times[0].tv_sec;
        tv[0].tv_usec = (int)(times[0].tv_nsec / 1000);
        tv[1].tv_sec = times[1].tv_sec;
        tv[1].tv_usec = (int)(times[1].tv_nsec / 1000);
        return futimes(fd, tv);
    }
    return futimes(fd, NULL);
}

/* utimensat - added 10.13 */
int utimensat(int fd, const char *path, const struct timespec times[2], int flag) {
    (void)fd; (void)flag;
    struct timeval tv[2];
    if (times) {
        tv[0].tv_sec = times[0].tv_sec;
        tv[0].tv_usec = (int)(times[0].tv_nsec / 1000);
        tv[1].tv_sec = times[1].tv_sec;
        tv[1].tv_usec = (int)(times[1].tv_nsec / 1000);
        return utimes(path, tv);
    }
    return utimes(path, NULL);
}

📝 Write stub_system.c


/Users/Jonathan/Downloads/Celeste64-v1.1.0-macOS-x64/compat/stub_system.c


/*
 * System compatibility shim for macOS 10.9.
 * Provides stub implementations of functions added in macOS 10.10+
 * that the .NET 8 runtime references. MacPorts Legacy Support handles
 * the POSIX functions (clock_gettime, fstatat, etc.).
 * This shim covers Security framework, CommonCrypto, and other gaps.
 */

#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdarg.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <syslog.h>
#include <Security/Security.h>

/* ============================================================
 * syslog$DARWIN_EXTSN - newer ABI variant
 * ============================================================ */
void syslog_darwin_extsn(int priority, const char *message, ...)
    __asm("_syslog$DARWIN_EXTSN");
void syslog_darwin_extsn(int priority, const char *message, ...) {
    va_list ap;
    va_start(ap, message);
    vsyslog(priority, message, ap);
    va_end(ap);
}

/* ============================================================
 * CommonCrypto - CCRandomGenerateBytes (added 10.10)
 * ============================================================ */
int CCRandomGenerateBytes(void *bytes, size_t count) {
    int fd = open("/dev/urandom", O_RDONLY);
    if (fd < 0) return -1;
    ssize_t r = read(fd, bytes, count);
    close(fd);
    return (r == (ssize_t)count) ? 0 : -1;
}

/* ============================================================
 * Security framework - SecKey functions (added 10.12+)
 * ============================================================ */

#define STUB_UNIMPLEMENTED (-4)

CFDataRef SecKeyCopyExternalRepresentation(SecKeyRef key, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

SecKeyRef SecKeyCreateWithData(CFDataRef keyData, CFDictionaryRef attributes, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)keyData; (void)attributes;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

SecKeyRef SecKeyCreateRandomKey(CFDictionaryRef parameters, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)parameters;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

CFDataRef SecKeyCreateSignature(SecKeyRef key, SecPadding algorithm,
                                CFDataRef dataToSign, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key; (void)algorithm; (void)dataToSign;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

Boolean SecKeyVerifySignature(SecKeyRef key, SecPadding algorithm,
                              CFDataRef signedData, CFDataRef signature,
                              CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key; (void)algorithm; (void)signedData; (void)signature;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return false;
}

CFDataRef SecKeyCreateEncryptedData(SecKeyRef key, SecPadding algorithm,
                                    CFDataRef plaintext, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key; (void)algorithm; (void)plaintext;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

CFDataRef SecKeyCreateDecryptedData(SecKeyRef key, SecPadding algorithm,
                                    CFDataRef ciphertext, CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)key; (void)algorithm; (void)ciphertext;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

SecKeyRef SecKeyCopyPublicKey(SecKeyRef key) {
    (void)key;
    return NULL;
}

CFDictionaryRef SecKeyCopyAttributes(SecKeyRef key) {
    (void)key;
    return NULL;
}

CFDataRef SecKeyCopyKeyExchangeResult(SecKeyRef publicKey, void *algorithm,
                                      SecKeyRef parameters, CFDictionaryRef requestedSize,
                                      CFErrorRef *error) {
    (void)publicKey; (void)algorithm; (void)parameters; (void)requestedSize;
    if (error) *error = NULL;
    return NULL;
}

/* SecCertificateCopyKey - added 10.14 */
SecKeyRef SecCertificateCopyKey(SecCertificateRef certificate) {
    (void)certificate;
    return NULL;
}

/* ============================================================
 * SSL/TLS ALPN functions (added 10.13.4)
 * ============================================================ */

OSStatus SSLCopyALPNProtocols(void *context, CFArrayRef *protocols) {
    (void)context;
    if (protocols) *protocols = NULL;
    return STUB_UNIMPLEMENTED;
}

OSStatus SSLSetALPNProtocols(void *context, CFArrayRef protocols) {
    (void)context; (void)protocols;
    return STUB_UNIMPLEMENTED;

📝 Write run_celeste64.sh


/Users/Jonathan/Downloads/Celeste64-v1.1.0-macOS-x64/run_celeste64.sh


#!/bin/bash
# Celeste64 launcher for macOS 10.9 compatibility
# Uses stub libraries for missing frameworks and system symbols

DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "$0")" && pwd)"

# Redirect missing framework/library loads to local stubs
export DYLD_FRAMEWORK_PATH="$DIR/compat:${DYLD_FRAMEWORK_PATH}"
export DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH="$DIR/compat/swift:${DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH}"

# Force flat namespace so shims can provide missing system symbols
export DYLD_FORCE_FLAT_NAMESPACE=1

# Insert MacPorts Legacy Support (clock_gettime, fstatat, etc.)
# and our custom compat shim (Security stubs, syslog, CCRandom)
export DYLD_INSERT_LIBRARIES="/usr/local/lib/libMacportsLegacySupport.dylib:$DIR/compat/libcompat.dylib"

exec "$DIR/Celeste64" "$@"

    33→int CCRandomGenerateBytes(void *bytes, size_t count) {
    34→    int fd = open("/dev/urandom", O_RDONLY);
    35→    if (fd < 0) return -1;
    36→    ssize_t r = read(fd, bytes, count);
    37→    close(fd);
    38→    return (r == (ssize_t)count) ? 0 : -1;
    39→}

/* ============================================================
 * syslog$DARWIN_EXTSN - newer ABI variant
 * ============================================================ */


+
/* ============================================================
 * thread_get_register_pointer_values (added ~10.11)
 * Used by .NET GC to scan thread registers for managed pointers.
 * ============================================================ */
kern_return_t thread_get_register_pointer_values(
    thread_read_t thread, uintptr_t *sp, size_t *count,
    uintptr_t *register_values)
{
    x86_thread_state64_t state;
    mach_msg_type_number_t state_count = x86_THREAD_STATE64_COUNT;
    kern_return_t kr = thread_get_state(thread, x86_THREAD_STATE64,
                                        (thread_state_t)&state, &state_count);
    if (kr != KERN_SUCCESS) return kr;

    if (sp) *sp = state.__rsp;

    /* Return all general-purpose registers that could hold pointers */
    if (register_values && count) {
        size_t i = 0;
        register_values[i++] = state.__rax;
        register_values[i++] = state.__rbx;
        register_values[i++] = state.__rcx;
        register_values[i++] = state.__rdx;
        register_values[i++] = state.__rdi;
        register_values[i++] = state.__rsi;
        register_values[i++] = state.__rbp;
        register_values[i++] = state.__r8;
        register_values[i++] = state.__r9;
        register_values[i++] = state.__r10;
        register_values[i++] = state.__r11;
        register_values[i++] = state.__r12;
        register_values[i++] = state.__r13;
        register_values[i++] = state.__r14;
        register_values[i++] = state.__r15;
        register_values[i++] = state.__rip;
        *count = i;
    }
    return KERN_SUCCESS;
}

/* ============================================================
 * syslog$DARWIN_EXTSN - newer ABI variant
 * ============================================================ */

/*
 * Stub CryptoKit framework for macOS 10.9 compatibility.
 * Exports Swift-mangled symbols with exact linker names via __asm__.
 */

#include <stdlib.h>

static char _stub_data[4096] __attribute__((aligned(16)));

/* Helper: define a stub function with the exact asm symbol name */
#define STUB_FUNC(csym, asmsym) \
    void csym(void) __asm__(asmsym); \
    void csym(void) { abort(); }

/* Helper: define a stub data symbol with the exact asm symbol name */
#define STUB_DATA(csym, asmsym) \
    void *csym __asm__(asmsym) __attribute__((visibility("default"))) = (void*)_stub_data;

/* ChaChaPoly */
STUB_FUNC(ck1, "_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO4open_5using14authenticating10Foundation4DataVAC9SealedBoxV_AA12SymmetricKeyVxtKAG0I8ProtocolRzlFZ")
STUB_FUNC(ck2, "_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO4seal_5using5nonce14authenticatingAC9SealedBoxVx_AA12SymmetricKeyVAC5NonceVSgq_tK10Foundation12DataProtocolRzAoPR_r0_lFZ")
STUB_FUNC(ck3, "_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO5NonceV4dataAEx_tKc10Foundation12DataProtocolRzlufC")
STUB_FUNC(ck4, "_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO5NonceVMa")
STUB_DATA(ck5, "_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO5NonceVMn")
STUB_FUNC(ck6, "_$s9CryptoKit03ChaC4PolyO9SealedBoxV10ciphertext10Foundation4DataVvg")

STUB_FUNC(ck10, "_$s9CryptoKit0aB5ErrorOMa")

/* ============================================================
 * ObjC runtime - objc_alloc_init (added ~10.14.4 / Xcode 10.2)
 * Combines [cls alloc] and [obj init] in one call.
 * ============================================================ */
id objc_alloc_init(Class cls) {
    id obj = ((id(*)(Class, SEL))objc_msgSend)(cls, sel_getUid("alloc"));
    return ((id(*)(id, SEL))objc_msgSend)(obj, sel_getUid("init"));
}

Tool reply2026-03-09T01:34:44.355Z
       -l <script-language>
       --script-language <script-language>
            Tells the debugger to use the specified scripting language for
            user-defined scripts, rather than the default.  Valid scripting
            languages that can be specified include Python, Perl, Ruby and Tcl.
            Currently only the Python extensions have been implemented.

       -d 
       --debug 
            Tells the debugger to print out extra information for debugging
            itself.

       -r 
       --repl 
            Runs lldb in REPL mode with a stub process.


  Notes:

       Multiple "-s" and "-o" options can be provided.  They will be processed from left to right in order, 
       with the source files and commands interleaved.  The same is true of the "-S" and "-O" options.
       The before file and after file sets can intermixed freely, the command parser will sort them out.
       The order of the file specifiers ("-c", "-f", etc.) is not significant in this regard.


       If you don't provide -f then the first argument will be the file to be debugged
       which means that 'lldb -- <filename> [<ARG1> [<ARG2>]]' also works.
       But remember to end the options with "--" if any of your arguments have a "-" in them.

/* ============================================================
 * thread_get_register_pointer_values (added ~10.11)
 * Used by .NET GC to scan thread registers for managed pointers.
 * ============================================================ */


+
/* ============================================================
 * ___chkstk_darwin - stack probe function (added ~10.12)
 * Called by compiler-generated code for large stack frames.
 * RAX contains the number of bytes to probe. This function
 * must touch each page to trigger guard page faults.
 * ============================================================ */
__asm__(
    ".globl ____chkstk_darwin\n"
    "____chkstk_darwin:\n"
    "  pushq  %rcx\n"
    "  pushq  %rax\n"
    "  cmpq   $0x1000, %rax\n"
    "  leaq   24(%rsp), %rcx\n"   /* rcx = original rsp */
    "  jb     .Ldone\n"
    ".Lloop:\n"
    "  subq   $0x1000, %rcx\n"
    "  testq  %rcx, (%rcx)\n"     /* probe the page */
    "  subq   $0x1000, %rax\n"
    "  cmpq   $0x1000, %rax\n"
    "  ja     .Lloop\n"
    ".Ldone:\n"
    "  subq   %rax, %rcx\n"
    "  testq  %rcx, (%rcx)\n"     /* probe last partial page */
    "  popq   %rax\n"
    "  popq   %rcx\n"
    "  retq\n"
);

/* ============================================================
 * thread_get_register_pointer_values (added ~10.11)
 * Used by .NET GC to scan thread registers for managed pointers.
 * ============================================================ */

/* ============================================================
 * mmap wrapper - strip MAP_JIT flag (0x0800, added 10.14)
 * The .NET runtime uses MAP_JIT for JIT code pages.
 * On 10.9 this flag doesn't exist and causes mmap to fail.
 * We strip it and call the real mmap.
 * ============================================================ */
#ifndef MAP_JIT
#define MAP_JIT 0x0800
#endif

/* We need to call the real mmap from libc. Since we're in flat namespace,
 * we can't easily call the real one by name. Instead, use syscall. */
#include <sys/syscall.h>

/* mmap syscall number on macOS x86_64 */
void *mmap(void *addr, size_t len, int prot, int flags, int fd, off_t offset) {
    /* Strip MAP_JIT flag - not supported on 10.9 */
    flags &= ~MAP_JIT;
    /* Use syscall to call the kernel mmap directly */
    return (void *)syscall(SYS_mmap, addr, len, prot, flags, fd, offset);
}

/* ============================================================
 * pthread_jit_write_protect_np (added macOS 11.0)
 * On x86_64, this is a no-op. On ARM it toggles W^X.
 * ============================================================ */
void pthread_jit_write_protect_np(int enabled) {
    (void)enabled;
    /* No-op on x86_64 */
}

/* We need to call the real mmap from libc. Since we're in flat namespace,
 * we can't easily call the real one by name. Instead, use syscall. */
#include <sys/syscall.h>

/* mmap syscall number on macOS x86_64 */
void *mmap(void *addr, size_t len, int prot, int flags, int fd, off_t offset) {
    /* Strip MAP_JIT flag - not supported on 10.9 */
    flags &= ~MAP_JIT;
    /* Use syscall to call the kernel mmap directly */
    return (void *)(uintptr_t)syscall(SYS_mmap, addr, len, prot, flags, fd, offset);
}


+
/* Use inline assembly to make the mmap syscall directly, preserving
 * the full 64-bit return value that C's syscall() truncates to int. */

/* macOS BSD syscall class = 0x2000000, mmap = 197 */
#define SYSCALL_MMAP (0x2000000 + 197)

void *mmap(void *addr, size_t len, int prot, int flags, int fd, off_t offset) {
    /* Strip MAP_JIT flag - not supported on 10.9 */
    flags &= ~MAP_JIT;

    void *result;
    __asm__ __volatile__ (
        "movq %1, %%rdi\n\t"
        "movq %2, %%rsi\n\t"
        "movl %3, %%edx\n\t"
        "movl %4, %%ecx\n\t"    /* r10 for syscall, but we set rcx */
        "movl %5, %%r8d\n\t"
        "movq %6, %%r9\n\t"
        "movl %7, %%eax\n\t"
        "movq %%rcx, %%r10\n\t" /* syscall uses r10 instead of rcx */
        "syscall\n\t"
        "jnc 1f\n\t"           /* if carry not set, success */
        "movq $-1, %%rax\n\t"  /* on error, return MAP_FAILED (-1) */
        "1:\n\t"
        : "=a"(result)
        : "r"(addr), "r"(len), "r"(prot), "r"(flags), "r"(fd), "r"((long)offset),
          "i"(SYSCALL_MMAP)
        : "rdi", "rsi", "rdx", "rcx", "r8", "r9", "r10", "r11", "cc", "memory"
    );
    return result;
}

−
/* Use inline assembly to make the mmap syscall directly, preserving
 * the full 64-bit return value that C's syscall() truncates to int. */

/* macOS BSD syscall class = 0x2000000, mmap = 197 */
#define SYSCALL_MMAP (0x2000000 + 197)

void *mmap(void *addr, size_t len, int prot, int flags, int fd, off_t offset) {
    /* Strip MAP_JIT flag - not supported on 10.9 */
    flags &= ~MAP_JIT;

    void *result;
    __asm__ __volatile__ (
        "movq %1, %%rdi\n\t"
        "movq %2, %%rsi\n\t"
        "movl %3, %%edx\n\t"
        "movl %4, %%ecx\n\t"    /* r10 for syscall, but we set rcx */
        "movl %5, %%r8d\n\t"
        "movq %6, %%r9\n\t"
        "movl %7, %%eax\n\t"
        "movq %%rcx, %%r10\n\t" /* syscall uses r10 instead of rcx */
        "syscall\n\t"
        "jnc 1f\n\t"           /* if carry not set, success */
        "movq $-1, %%rax\n\t"  /* on error, return MAP_FAILED (-1) */
        "1:\n\t"
        : "=a"(result)
        : "r"(addr), "r"(len), "r"(prot), "r"(flags), "r"(fd), "r"((long)offset),
          "i"(SYSCALL_MMAP)
        : "rdi", "rsi", "rdx", "rcx", "r8", "r9", "r10", "r11", "cc", "memory"
    );
    return result;
}


+
/* Call the kernel's raw __mmap (from libsystem_kernel) which bypasses
 * our override and preserves the 64-bit return value. */
extern void *__mmap(void *addr, size_t len, int prot, int flags, int fd, off_t offset);

void *mmap(void *addr, size_t len, int prot, int flags, int fd, off_t offset) {
    /* Strip MAP_JIT flag - not supported on 10.9 */
    flags &= ~MAP_JIT;
    return __mmap(addr, len, prot, flags, fd, offset);
}

void *mmap(void *addr, size_t len, int prot, int flags, int fd, off_t offset) {
    int had_jit = (flags & MAP_JIT);
    /* Strip MAP_JIT flag - not supported on 10.9 */
    flags &= ~MAP_JIT;
    void *result = __mmap(addr, len, prot, flags, fd, offset);
    if (had_jit) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[compat] mmap(len=%zu, prot=%d, flags=0x%x): stripped MAP_JIT -> %p\n",
                len, prot, flags, result);
    }
    return result;
}

Assistant2026-03-09T01:48:43.394Z


📝 Write patch_macho.c


/Users/Jonathan/Downloads/Celeste64-v1.1.0-macOS-x64/compat/patch_macho.c


/*
 * Patches a Mach-O binary to convert newer load commands to formats
 * compatible with macOS 10.9's dyld.
 *
 * Specifically:
 * - LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS (0x80000033) -> cleared LC_REQ_DYLD bit
 * - LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE (0x80000034) -> cleared LC_REQ_DYLD bit
 * - LC_BUILD_VERSION (0x32) -> converted to LC_VERSION_MIN_MACOSX (0x24)
 *
 * Also processes chained fixups to generate traditional rebase/bind info
 * and creates LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY from the exports trie.
 */

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdint.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <sys/mman.h>
#include <mach-o/loader.h>
#include <mach-o/nlist.h>

#define LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE    0x80000034
#define LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS  0x80000033
#define LC_BUILD_VERSION_CMD    0x00000032
#define LC_REQ_DYLD             0x80000000

/* Chained fixups structures */
struct dyld_chained_fixups_header {
    uint32_t fixups_version;
    uint32_t starts_offset;
    uint32_t imports_offset;
    uint32_t symbols_offset;
    uint32_t imports_count;
    uint32_t imports_format;
    uint32_t symbols_format;
};

struct dyld_chained_starts_in_image {
    uint32_t seg_count;
    uint32_t seg_info_offset[]; /* offsets from start of this struct */
};

struct dyld_chained_starts_in_segment {
    uint32_t size;
    uint16_t page_size;
    uint16_t pointer_format;
    uint64_t segment_offset;
    uint32_t max_valid_pointer;
    uint16_t page_count;
    uint16_t page_start[];
};

/* Chained import formats */
struct dyld_chained_import {
    uint32_t lib_ordinal : 8;
    uint32_t weak_import : 1;
    uint32_t name_offset : 23;
};

/* Pointer format constants */
#define DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_64           2
#define DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_64_OFFSET    6
#define DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_64_KERNEL_CACHE 1

#define DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_START_NONE   0xFFFF
#define DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_START_MULTI  0x8000

/* Rebase opcode constants */
#define REBASE_TYPE_POINTER                         1
#define REBASE_OPCODE_MASK                          0xF0
#define REBASE_IMMEDIATE_MASK                       0x0F
#define REBASE_OPCODE_DONE                          0x00
#define REBASE_OPCODE_SET_TYPE_IMM                  0x10
#define REBASE_OPCODE_SET_SEGMENT_AND_OFFSET_ULEB   0x20
#define REBASE_OPCODE_ADD_ADDR_ULEB                 0x30
#define REBASE_OPCODE_DO_REBASE_ULEB_TIMES          0x50
#define REBASE_OPCODE_DO_REBASE_IMM_TIMES           0xA0
#define REBASE_OPCODE_DO_REBASE_ADD_ADDR_ULEB       0x80

/* Bind opcode constants */
#define BIND_TYPE_POINTER                           1
#define BIND_OPCODE_DONE                            0x00
#define BIND_OPCODE_SET_DYLIB_ORDINAL_IMM           0x10
#define BIND_OPCODE_SET_DYLIB_ORDINAL_ULEB          0x20
#define BIND_OPCODE_SET_SYMBOL_FLAGS_IMM            0x40
#define BIND_OPCODE_SET_TYPE_IMM                    0x50
#define BIND_OPCODE_SET_SEGMENT_AND_OFFSET_ULEB     0x70
#define BIND_OPCODE_DO_BIND                         0x90

static int write_uleb128(uint8_t *buf, uint64_t value) {
    int count = 0;
    do {
        uint8_t byte = value & 0x7F;
        value >>= 7;
        if (value) byte |= 0x80;
        buf[count++] = byte;
    } while (value);
    return count;
}

int main(int argc, char **argv) {
    if (argc != 3) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Usage: %s <input.dylib> <output.dylib>\n", argv[0]);
        return 1;
    }

    /* Read input file */
    int fd = open(argv[1], O_RDONLY);
    if (fd < 0) { perror("open"); return 1; }
    struct stat st;
    fstat(fd, &st);
    size_t filesize = st.st_size;

    uint8_t *buf = malloc(filesize + 1024*1024); /* extra space for new data */
    if (!buf) { perror("malloc"); return 1; }
    read(fd, buf, filesize);
    close(fd);

    struct mach_header_64 *hdr = (struct mach_header_64 *)buf;
    if (hdr->magic != MH_MAGIC_64) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Not a 64-bit Mach-O\n");
        return 1;
    }

    /* Scan load commands to find what we need */
    uint8_t *lc_ptr = buf + sizeof(struct mach_header_64);
    uint32_t exports_off = 0, exports_size = 0;
    uint32_t fixups_off = 0, fixups_size = 0;
    struct load_command *lc_exports_trie = NULL;
    struct load_command *lc_chained_fixups = NULL;
    struct load_command *lc_build_version = NULL;
    struct segment_command_64 *segments[16];
    int nsegments = 0;

    /* Also find LC_ID_DYLIB for the load order list */
    struct load_command *lc_iter = (struct load_command *)lc_ptr;
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < hdr->ncmds; i++) {
        if (lc_iter->cmd == LC_SEGMENT_64) {
            segments[nsegments++] = (struct segment_command_64 *)lc_iter;
        } else if (lc_iter->cmd == LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE) {
            lc_exports_trie = lc_iter;
            uint32_t *data = (uint32_t *)lc_iter;
            exports_off = data[2];
            exports_size = data[3];
            printf("Found LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE: offset=%u size=%u\n", exports_off, exports_size);
        } else if (lc_iter->cmd == LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS) {
            lc_chained_fixups = lc_iter;
            uint32_t *data = (uint32_t *)lc_iter;
            fixups_off = data[2];
            fixups_size = data[3];
            printf("Found LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS: offset=%u size=%u\n", fixups_off, fixups_size);
        } else if (lc_iter->cmd == LC_BUILD_VERSION_CMD) {
            lc_build_version = lc_iter;
        }
        lc_iter = (struct load_command *)((uint8_t *)lc_iter + lc_iter->cmdsize);
    }

    if (!lc_chained_fixups || !lc_exports_trie) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Missing required load commands\n");
        return 1;
    }

    /* Parse chained fixups and generate rebase/bind opcodes */
    struct dyld_chained_fixups_header *fixhdr = (struct dyld_chained_fixups_header *)(buf + fixups_off);
    struct dyld_chained_starts_in_image *starts = (struct dyld_chained_starts_in_image *)(buf + fixups_off + fixhdr->starts_offset);

    /* Import table for bind operations */
    struct dyld_chained_import *imports = (struct dyld_chained_import *)(buf + fixups_off + fixhdr->imports_offset);
    char *symbols_pool = (char *)(buf + fixups_off + fixhdr->symbols_offset);

    printf("Fixups: version=%u, imports_count=%u, imports_format=%u\n",
           fixhdr->fixups_version, fixhdr->imports_count, fixhdr->imports_format);
    printf("Segments: %u\n", starts->seg_count);

    /* Allocate buffers for rebase and bind opcodes */
    uint8_t *rebase_buf = malloc(1024*1024);
    uint8_t *bind_buf = malloc(1024*1024);
    int rebase_pos = 0, bind_pos = 0;

    /* Start rebase stream */
    rebase_buf[rebase_pos++] = REBASE_OPCODE_SET_TYPE_IMM | REBASE_TYPE_POINTER;

    /* Start bind stream */
    bind_buf[bind_pos++] = BIND_OPCODE_SET_TYPE_IMM | BIND_TYPE_POINTER;

    for (uint32_t seg_idx = 0; seg_idx < starts->seg_count; seg_idx++) {
        uint32_t seg_info_off = starts->seg_info_offset[seg_idx];
        if (seg_info_off == 0) continue;

        struct dyld_chained_starts_in_segment *seg_starts =
            (struct dyld_chained_starts_in_segment *)((uint8_t *)starts + seg_info_off);

        printf("  Segment %u: page_size=%u, pointer_format=%u, pages=%u, seg_off=0x%llx\n",
               seg_idx, seg_starts->page_size, seg_starts->pointer_format,
               seg_starts->page_count, seg_starts->segment_offset);

        uint16_t ptr_fmt = seg_starts->pointer_format;
        uint64_t seg_file_off = segments[seg_idx]->fileoff;

        for (uint16_t page = 0; page < seg_starts->page_count; page++) {
            uint16_t page_start = seg_starts->page_start[page];
            if (page_start == DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_START_NONE) continue;

            uint64_t page_off = (uint64_t)page * seg_starts->page_size;
            uint64_t chain_off = seg_starts->segment_offset + page_off + page_start;
            uint64_t seg_off_in_seg = page_off + page_start;

            /* Walk the chain */
            while (1) {
                uint64_t *fixup_ptr = (uint64_t *)(buf + seg_file_off + seg_off_in_seg);
                uint64_t raw = *fixup_ptr;

                int is_bind;
                uint64_t next_delta;

                if (ptr_fmt == DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_64 || ptr_fmt == DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_64_OFFSET) {
                    /* 64-bit pointer format:
                     * Bit 63: 0=rebase, 1=bind
                     * Rebase: bits [51:0] = target, bits [62:52] = high8 (DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_64) or just target for _OFFSET
                     * Bind: bits [23:0] = ordinal, bits [31:24] = addend, bits [51:32] = reserved
                     * Both: bits [62:52] contain next delta (for PTR_64) / [51:36] for _OFFSET
                     */
                    is_bind = (raw >> 63) & 1;
                    if (ptr_fmt == DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_64) {
                        next_delta = (raw >> 51) & 0x7FF;  /* bits [61:51], 11 bits */
                        next_delta *= 4;
                    } else {
                        next_delta = (raw >> 36) & 0x7FFF; /* bits [50:36], 15 bits */
                        next_delta *= 4;
                    }

                    if (is_bind) {
                        uint32_t ordinal = raw & 0xFFFFFF;
                        int64_t addend = (int64_t)(int8_t)((raw >> 24) & 0xFF);
                        (void)addend;

                        if (ordinal < fixhdr->imports_count) {
                            int lib_ord = imports[ordinal].lib_ordinal;
                            char *sym_name = symbols_pool + imports[ordinal].name_offset;

                            /* Emit bind opcodes */
                            if (lib_ord > 0 && lib_ord < 16) {
                                bind_buf[bind_pos++] = BIND_OPCODE_SET_DYLIB_ORDINAL_IMM | lib_ord;
                            } else {
                                bind_buf[bind_pos++] = BIND_OPCODE_SET_DYLIB_ORDINAL_ULEB;
                                bind_pos += write_uleb128(bind_buf + bind_pos, lib_ord);
                            }
                            int sym_len = strlen(sym_name);
                            int flags = imports[ordinal].weak_import ? 1 : 0;
                            bind_buf[bind_pos++] = BIND_OPCODE_SET_SYMBOL_FLAGS_IMM | flags;
                            memcpy(bind_buf + bind_pos, sym_name, sym_len + 1);
                            bind_pos += sym_len + 1;
                            bind_buf[bind_pos++] = BIND_OPCODE_SET_SEGMENT_AND_OFFSET_ULEB | seg_idx;
                            bind_pos += write_uleb128(bind_buf + bind_pos, seg_off_in_seg);
                            bind_buf[bind_pos++] = BIND_OPCODE_DO_BIND;

                            /* Apply the bind fixup in-place: set to 0, dyld will fill it */
                            *fixup_ptr = 0;
                        }
                    } else {
                        /* Rebase: extract the target address */
                        uint64_t target;
                        if (ptr_fmt == DYLD_CHAINED_PTR_64) {
                            target = raw & 0x7FFFFFFFFFF; /* bits [42:0] */
                            uint8_t high8 = (raw >> 43) & 0xFF;
                            target |= (uint64_t)high8 << 56;
                        } else {
                            target = raw & 0xFFFFFFFFF; /* bits [35:0] */
                        }

                        /* Emit rebase opcode */
                        rebase_buf[rebase_pos++] = REBASE_OPCODE_SET_SEGMENT_AND_OFFSET_ULEB | seg_idx;
                        rebase_pos += write_uleb128(rebase_buf + rebase_pos, seg_off_in_seg);
                        rebase_buf[rebase_pos++] = REBASE_OPCODE_DO_REBASE_IMM_TIMES | 1;

                        /* Apply the rebase fixup in-place */
                        *fixup_ptr = target;
                    }
                } else {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Unsupported pointer format: %u\n", ptr_fmt);
                    return 1;
                }

                if (next_delta == 0) break;
                seg_off_in_seg += next_delta;
            }
        }
    }

    /* Terminate opcode streams */
    rebase_buf[rebase_pos++] = REBASE_OPCODE_DONE;
    bind_buf[bind_pos++] = BIND_OPCODE_DONE;

    printf("Generated %d bytes of rebase opcodes\n", rebase_pos);
    printf("Generated %d bytes of bind opcodes\n", bind_pos);

    /* Now we need to:
     * 1. Append rebase + bind data after the file
     * 2. Replace the two 16-byte commands with new LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY (48 bytes)
     *    We need 48 bytes but only have 32. We'll need to grow the header.
     *    Actually, we can repurpose the LC_BUILD_VERSION command (if present)
     *    to be LC_VERSION_MIN_MACOSX, which is smaller.
     *
     * Simpler approach: replace LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS (16 bytes) with a
     * zeroed-out placeholder, and repurpose LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE (16 bytes)
     * similarly. Then use the space from LC_BUILD_VERSION (probably 32+ bytes).
     *
     * Actually, the simplest: combine the two 16-byte commands into available
     * space. We can change the ncmds and sizeofcmds to add a new command.
     *
     * Even simpler: overwrite the LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS with the start of
     * LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY, let it overflow into LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE space,
     * and use LC_BUILD_VERSION for the remaining bytes. We have 16+16=32 bytes
     * from the two commands, but need 48.
     *
     * Let's check LC_BUILD_VERSION size.
     */

    /* Actually - let's take a different approach. Append the rebase/bind data at
     * the end of the file. For the load command, we'll:
     * 1. Replace LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE (16 bytes) + LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS (16 bytes)
     *    = 32 bytes with padding
     * 2. Replace LC_BUILD_VERSION (32+ bytes) with LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY (48 bytes)
     *    IF it's big enough, otherwise rearrange.
     *
     * Actually, simplest: the load commands area has some slack. Let me just
     * overwrite the two commands and decrease ncmds by 1 (removing one command
     * and replacing the other with the 48-byte LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY that overflows
     * into the now-freed space).
     */

    /* Step 1: Find positions of the two commands to replace */
    uint8_t *cmd5_pos = (uint8_t *)lc_exports_trie;
    uint8_t *cmd6_pos = (uint8_t *)lc_chained_fixups;

    /* Ensure they are adjacent (exports_trie then chained_fixups) */
    if (cmd6_pos != cmd5_pos + 16) {
        /* They might be in different order */
        if (cmd5_pos == cmd6_pos + 16) {
            /* Swap so exports_trie is first */
            uint8_t *tmp = cmd5_pos;
            cmd5_pos = cmd6_pos;
            cmd6_pos = tmp;
        } else {
            fprintf(stderr, "Commands not adjacent, need different strategy\n");
            return 1;
        }
    }

    /* We have 32 bytes of space (two 16-byte commands). We need 48 bytes for
     * LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY. Let's check if LC_BUILD_VERSION is right after and
     * can be absorbed. */
    uint8_t *after_cmd6 = cmd6_pos + 16;

    /* Append rebase and bind data at end of file */
    size_t rebase_file_off = filesize;
    /* Align to 8 bytes */
    rebase_file_off = (rebase_file_off + 7) & ~7;
    memcpy(buf + rebase_file_off, rebase_buf, rebase_pos);
    size_t bind_file_off = rebase_file_off + rebase_pos;
    bind_file_off = (bind_file_off + 7) & ~7;
    memcpy(buf + bind_file_off, bind_buf, bind_pos);
    size_t new_filesize = bind_file_off + bind_pos;

    /* Now patch the load commands.
     * Strategy: convert the first 16-byte command to LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY (48 bytes)
     * which will overflow into the second 16-byte command space (32 bytes used of 48).
     * Shift remaining load commands down by 16 bytes (48 - 32 = 16 extra needed).
     * Actually this is complex. Let me use a simpler strategy:
     *
     * Alternative: just create LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY as a new command by using
     * space from removing two commands (-32) and adding one (+48) = net +16 bytes.
     * Move remaining commands up. Need to shift from cmd6_pos+16 onward by
     * expanding by 16 bytes... that's backward shifting.
     *
     * SIMPLEST: Delete both old commands. Add LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY at the end
     * of the load commands. ncmds goes from N to N-2+1 = N-1.
     */

    /* Calculate where load commands end */
    uint8_t *lcmds_start = buf + sizeof(struct mach_header_64);
    uint8_t *lcmds_end = lcmds_start + hdr->sizeofcmds;

    /* Remove the two old commands by shifting everything after them */
    /* Remove exports_trie (at cmd5_pos, 16 bytes) */
    size_t remaining_after_5 = lcmds_end - (cmd5_pos + 16);
    memmove(cmd5_pos, cmd5_pos + 16, remaining_after_5);
    lcmds_end -= 16;
    hdr->ncmds--;
    hdr->sizeofcmds -= 16;

    /* Now find chained_fixups again (it shifted by 16) */
    cmd6_pos -= 16; /* since we removed 16 bytes before it */
    if (cmd6_pos >= cmd5_pos) {
        /* Only shifted if it was after cmd5 */
    } else {
        cmd6_pos += 16; /* was before, didn't shift */
    }
    /* Actually, let's just re-find it */
    lc_iter = (struct load_command *)lcmds_start;
    cmd6_pos = NULL;
    lc_build_version = NULL;
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < hdr->ncmds; i++) {
        if (lc_iter->cmd == LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS) {
            cmd6_pos = (uint8_t *)lc_iter;
        } else if (lc_iter->cmd == LC_BUILD_VERSION_CMD) {
            lc_build_version = lc_iter;
        }
        lc_iter = (struct load_command *)((uint8_t *)lc_iter + lc_iter->cmdsize);
    }

    if (cmd6_pos) {
        remaining_after_5 = lcmds_end - (cmd6_pos + 16);
        memmove(cmd6_pos, cmd6_pos + 16, remaining_after_5);
        lcmds_end -= 16;
        hdr->ncmds--;
        hdr->sizeofcmds -= 16;
    }

    /* Also remove LC_BUILD_VERSION (unknown to 10.9 dyld, non-required so
     * it would be OK, but let's be safe) */
    if (lc_build_version) {
        /* Re-find it since pointers shifted */
        lc_iter = (struct load_command *)lcmds_start;
        for (uint32_t i = 0; i < hdr->ncmds; i++) {
            if (lc_iter->cmd == LC_BUILD_VERSION_CMD) {
                uint32_t cs = lc_iter->cmdsize;
                uint8_t *pos = (uint8_t *)lc_iter;
                size_t remaining = lcmds_end - (pos + cs);
                memmove(pos, pos + cs, remaining);
                lcmds_end -= cs;
                hdr->ncmds--;
                hdr->sizeofcmds -= cs;
                break;
            }
            lc_iter = (struct load_command *)((uint8_t *)lc_iter + lc_iter->cmdsize);
        }
    }

    /* Now append LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY at the end of load commands */
    /* Check if there's room (load commands must fit before first segment's data) */
    uint8_t *new_lcmds_end = lcmds_end;
    if (new_lcmds_end + 48 > buf + segments[0]->fileoff) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Warning: Not enough space for new load command in header!\n");
        /* In practice there should be space since we removed 32+ bytes */
    }

    struct dyld_info_command *dyld_info = (struct dyld_info_command *)new_lcmds_end;
    memset(dyld_info, 0, sizeof(struct dyld_info_command));
    dyld_info->cmd = LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY;
    dyld_info->cmdsize = sizeof(struct dyld_info_command); /* 48 */
    dyld_info->rebase_off = (uint32_t)rebase_file_off;
    dyld_info->rebase_size = rebase_pos;
    dyld_info->bind_off = (uint32_t)bind_file_off;
    dyld_info->bind_size = bind_pos;
    dyld_info->weak_bind_off = 0;
    dyld_info->weak_bind_size = 0;
    dyld_info->lazy_bind_off = 0;
    dyld_info->lazy_bind_size = 0;
    dyld_info->export_off = exports_off;
    dyld_info->export_size = exports_size;

    hdr->ncmds++;
    hdr->sizeofcmds += 48;

    printf("New load commands: ncmds=%u, sizeofcmds=%u\n", hdr->ncmds, hdr->sizeofcmds);
    printf("Wrote rebase at offset %zu (%d bytes)\n", rebase_file_off, rebase_pos);
    printf("Wrote bind at offset %zu (%d bytes)\n", bind_file_off, bind_pos);
    printf("Exports trie at offset %u (%u bytes)\n", exports_off, exports_size);

    /* Write output */
    fd = open(argv[2], O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_TRUNC, 0755);
    if (fd < 0) { perror("open output"); return 1; }
    write(fd, buf, new_filesize);
    close(fd);

    printf("Patched %s -> %s (%zu bytes)\n", argv[1], argv[2], new_filesize);

    free(rebase_buf);
    free(bind_buf);
    free(buf);
    return 0;
}

📝 Write patch_macho.c


/Users/Jonathan/Downloads/Celeste64-v1.1.0-macOS-x64/compat/patch_macho.c


/*
 * Convert a Mach-O dylib from chained fixups format (macOS 12+)
 * to traditional LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY format (macOS 10.6+).
 */

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdint.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <mach-o/loader.h>
#include <mach-o/nlist.h>

#define LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE    0x80000034
#define LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS  0x80000033
#define LC_BUILD_VERSION_CMD    0x00000032

/* Chained fixups structures (not in 10.9 headers) */
struct cf_header {
    uint32_t fixups_version;
    uint32_t starts_offset;
    uint32_t imports_offset;
    uint32_t symbols_offset;
    uint32_t imports_count;
    uint32_t imports_format;
    uint32_t symbols_format;
};

struct cf_starts_image {
    uint32_t seg_count;
    uint32_t seg_info_offset[];
};

struct cf_starts_seg {
    uint32_t size;
    uint16_t page_size;
    uint16_t pointer_format;
    uint64_t segment_offset;
    uint32_t max_valid_pointer;
    uint16_t page_count;
    uint16_t page_start[];
};

struct cf_import {
    uint32_t bits; /* lib_ordinal:8, weak_import:1, name_offset:23 */
};

#define CF_PTR_64        2
#define CF_PTR_64_OFFSET 6
#define CF_START_NONE    0xFFFF

/* Dynamic buffer for opcodes */
struct opbuf {
    uint8_t *data;
    size_t len, cap;
};

static void ob_init(struct opbuf *b) { b->data = malloc(1024*1024); b->len = 0; b->cap = 1024*1024; }
static void ob_byte(struct opbuf *b, uint8_t v) { b->data[b->len++] = v; }
static void ob_uleb(struct opbuf *b, uint64_t v) {
    do { uint8_t byte = v & 0x7F; v >>= 7; if (v) byte |= 0x80; ob_byte(b, byte); } while (v);
}
static void ob_str(struct opbuf *b, const char *s) {
    while (*s) ob_byte(b, *s++);
    ob_byte(b, 0);
}

int main(int argc, char **argv) {
    if (argc != 3) { fprintf(stderr, "Usage: %s input output\n", argv[0]); return 1; }

    /* Read file */
    int fd = open(argv[1], O_RDONLY);
    struct stat st; fstat(fd, &st);
    size_t fsize = st.st_size;
    uint8_t *buf = malloc(fsize + 2*1024*1024);
    if (read(fd, buf, fsize) != (ssize_t)fsize) { perror("read"); return 1; }
    close(fd);

    struct mach_header_64 *hdr = (struct mach_header_64 *)buf;
    if (hdr->magic != MH_MAGIC_64) { fprintf(stderr, "Not 64-bit Mach-O (magic=0x%x)\n", hdr->magic); return 1; }

    /* Collect segments and find special load commands */
    struct segment_command_64 *segs[32] = {0};
    int nsegs = 0;
    uint32_t exports_off = 0, exports_size = 0;
    uint32_t fixups_off = 0, fixups_size = 0;

    /* Track positions and sizes of commands to remove */
    struct { uint8_t *pos; uint32_t size; } to_remove[4];
    int n_remove = 0;

    uint8_t *lcp = buf + sizeof(struct mach_header_64);
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < hdr->ncmds; i++) {
        struct load_command *lc = (struct load_command *)lcp;
        if (lc->cmd == LC_SEGMENT_64) {
            segs[nsegs++] = (struct segment_command_64 *)lc;
        } else if (lc->cmd == LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE) {
            uint32_t *d = (uint32_t *)lc;
            exports_off = d[2]; exports_size = d[3];
            to_remove[n_remove++] = (typeof(to_remove[0])){lcp, lc->cmdsize};
            printf("Exports trie: off=%u size=%u\n", exports_off, exports_size);
        } else if (lc->cmd == LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS) {
            uint32_t *d = (uint32_t *)lc;
            fixups_off = d[2]; fixups_size = d[3];
            to_remove[n_remove++] = (typeof(to_remove[0])){lcp, lc->cmdsize};
            printf("Chained fixups: off=%u size=%u\n", fixups_off, fixups_size);
        } else if (lc->cmd == LC_BUILD_VERSION_CMD) {
            to_remove[n_remove++] = (typeof(to_remove[0])){lcp, lc->cmdsize};
        }
        lcp += lc->cmdsize;
    }

    if (!fixups_off) { fprintf(stderr, "No chained fixups found\n"); return 1; }
    printf("Found %d segments\n", nsegs);

    /* Parse chained fixups */
    struct cf_header *cfh = (struct cf_header *)(buf + fixups_off);
    struct cf_starts_image *csi = (struct cf_starts_image *)(buf + fixups_off + cfh->starts_offset);
    struct cf_import *imports = (struct cf_import *)(buf + fixups_off + cfh->imports_offset);
    char *sympool = (char *)(buf + fixups_off + cfh->symbols_offset);

    printf("Fixups v%u: %u imports, %u segs in starts\n",
           cfh->fixups_version, cfh->imports_count, csi->seg_count);

    /* Generate rebase and bind opcodes */
    struct opbuf rebase, bind;
    ob_init(&rebase); ob_init(&bind);
    ob_byte(&rebase, REBASE_OPCODE_SET_TYPE_IMM | REBASE_TYPE_POINTER);
    ob_byte(&bind, BIND_OPCODE_SET_TYPE_IMM | BIND_TYPE_POINTER);

    int total_rebases = 0, total_binds = 0;

    for (uint32_t si = 0; si < csi->seg_count && si < (uint32_t)nsegs; si++) {
        if (csi->seg_info_offset[si] == 0) continue;
        struct cf_starts_seg *ss = (struct cf_starts_seg *)((uint8_t *)csi + csi->seg_info_offset[si]);
        printf("  Seg %u (%s): fmt=%u pages=%u segoff=0x%llx\n",
               si, segs[si]->segname, ss->pointer_format, ss->page_count, ss->segment_offset);

        for (uint16_t pg = 0; pg < ss->page_count; pg++) {
            uint16_t ps = ss->page_start[pg];
            if (ps == CF_START_NONE) continue;

            uint64_t off_in_seg = (uint64_t)pg * ss->page_size + ps;

            while (1) {
                uint64_t file_pos = segs[si]->fileoff + off_in_seg;
                if (file_pos + 8 > fsize) {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Fixup out of bounds at seg %u off 0x%llx\n", si, off_in_seg);
                    break;
                }
                uint64_t *ptr = (uint64_t *)(buf + file_pos);
                uint64_t raw = *ptr;
                int is_bind = (raw >> 63) & 1;
                uint32_t next;

                if (ss->pointer_format == CF_PTR_64) {
                    next = ((raw >> 51) & 0xFFF) * 4;
                } else if (ss->pointer_format == CF_PTR_64_OFFSET) {
                    next = ((raw >> 36) & 0x7FFF) * 4;
                } else {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Unknown ptr format %u\n", ss->pointer_format);
                    return 1;
                }

                if (is_bind) {
                    uint32_t ordinal = raw & 0xFFFFFF;
                    if (ordinal >= cfh->imports_count) {
                        fprintf(stderr, "Bad ordinal %u\n", ordinal);
                        break;
                    }
                    uint32_t bits = imports[ordinal].bits;
                    int lib_ord = bits & 0xFF;
                    /* Handle signed 8-bit lib ordinal */
                    if (lib_ord > 127) lib_ord -= 256;
                    int weak = (bits >> 8) & 1;
                    uint32_t name_off = bits >> 9;
                    char *sym = sympool + name_off;

                    /* Emit bind opcodes */
                    if (lib_ord >= 0 && lib_ord < 16) {
                        ob_byte(&bind, BIND_OPCODE_SET_DYLIB_ORDINAL_IMM | lib_ord);
                    } else {
                        ob_byte(&bind, BIND_OPCODE_SET_DYLIB_ORDINAL_ULEB);
                        ob_uleb(&bind, (uint64_t)(int64_t)lib_ord);
                    }
                    ob_byte(&bind, BIND_OPCODE_SET_SYMBOL_TRAILING_FLAGS_IMM | (weak ? BIND_SYMBOL_FLAGS_WEAK_IMPORT : 0));
                    ob_str(&bind, sym);
                    ob_byte(&bind, BIND_OPCODE_SET_SEGMENT_AND_OFFSET_ULEB | si);
                    ob_uleb(&bind, off_in_seg);
                    ob_byte(&bind, BIND_OPCODE_DO_BIND);

                    *ptr = 0; /* dyld will fill in */
                    total_binds++;
                } else {
                    /* Rebase */
                    uint64_t target;
                    if (ss->pointer_format == CF_PTR_64) {
                        target = raw & 0x7FFFFFFFFFF; /* bits [42:0] */
                        uint8_t high8 = (raw >> 43) & 0xFF;
                        target |= (uint64_t)high8 << 56;
                    } else {
                        target = raw & 0xFFFFFFFFF; /* bits [35:0] */
                    }

                    ob_byte(&rebase, REBASE_OPCODE_SET_SEGMENT_AND_OFFSET_ULEB | si);
                    ob_uleb(&rebase, off_in_seg);
                    ob_byte(&rebase, REBASE_OPCODE_DO_REBASE_IMM_TIMES | 1);

                    *ptr = target;
                    total_rebases++;
                }

                if (next == 0) break;
                off_in_seg += next;
            }
        }
    }

    ob_byte(&rebase, REBASE_OPCODE_DONE);
    ob_byte(&bind, BIND_OPCODE_DONE);
    printf("Processed %d rebases, %d binds\n", total_rebases, total_binds);

    /* Remove old commands from the header (process in reverse order to maintain positions) */
    /* Sort by position descending */
    for (int i = 0; i < n_remove - 1; i++) {
        for (int j = i + 1; j < n_remove; j++) {
            if (to_remove[j].pos > to_remove[i].pos) {
                typeof(to_remove[0]) tmp = to_remove[i];
                to_remove[i] = to_remove[j];
                to_remove[j] = tmp;
            }
        }
    }

    uint8_t *lcmds_end = buf + sizeof(struct mach_header_64) + hdr->sizeofcmds;
    for (int i = 0; i < n_remove; i++) {
        uint8_t *pos = to_remove[i].pos;
        uint32_t sz = to_remove[i].size;
        size_t tail = lcmds_end - (pos + sz);
        memmove(pos, pos + sz, tail);
        lcmds_end -= sz;
        hdr->ncmds--;
        hdr->sizeofcmds -= sz;
        printf("Removed cmd at %ld (size %u)\n", pos - buf, sz);
    }

    /* Add LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY */
    /* Append data at end of file (aligned) */
    size_t new_end = (fsize + 7) & ~7UL;
    uint32_t rebase_foff = (uint32_t)new_end;
    memcpy(buf + new_end, rebase.data, rebase.len);
    new_end += rebase.len;
    new_end = (new_end + 7) & ~7UL;
    uint32_t bind_foff = (uint32_t)new_end;
    memcpy(buf + new_end, bind.data, bind.len);
    new_end += bind.len;

    /* Check space for new load command */
    uint8_t *first_seg_data = buf + segs[0]->fileoff;
    if (lcmds_end + 48 > first_seg_data) {
        fprintf(stderr, "ERROR: No room for LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY (need 48 bytes, have %ld)\n",
                first_seg_data - lcmds_end);
        return 1;
    }

    struct dyld_info_command *di = (struct dyld_info_command *)lcmds_end;
    memset(di, 0, 48);
    di->cmd = LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY;
    di->cmdsize = 48;
    di->rebase_off = rebase_foff;
    di->rebase_size = (uint32_t)rebase.len;
    di->bind_off = bind_foff;
    di->bind_size = (uint32_t)bind.len;
    di->export_off = exports_off;
    di->export_size = exports_size;
    hdr->ncmds++;
    hdr->sizeofcmds += 48;

    printf("Added LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY: rebase=%u+%zu bind=%u+%zu exports=%u+%u\n",
           rebase_foff, rebase.len, bind_foff, bind.len, exports_off, exports_size);

    /* Write output */
    fd = open(argv[2], O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_TRUNC, 0755);
    if (fd < 0) { perror("create output"); return 1; }
    write(fd, buf, new_end);
    close(fd);
    printf("Wrote %s (%zu bytes)\n", argv[2], new_end);

    free(rebase.data); free(bind.data); free(buf);
    return 0;
}

Parse the chained fixups properly with Python
# Find the exact position of the chained fixups load command in the file
# The header is 32 bytes, then load commands follow
# Let me just search for the magic bytes 0x80000033
xxd /Users/Jonathan/Downloads/Celeste64-v1.1.0-macOS-x64/libFosterPlatform_x64.dylib | head -5
# Check what offset the load commands are at
python3 -c "
import struct, sys
with open('libFosterPlatform_x64.dylib', 'rb') as f:
    magic, cputype, cpusub, filetype, ncmds, sizeofcmds, flags, reserved = struct.unpack('<IIIIIIII', f.read(32))
    print(f'magic=0x{magic:08x} ncmds={ncmds} sizeofcmds={sizeofcmds}')
    off = 32
    for i in range(ncmds):
        f.seek(off)
        cmd, cmdsize = struct.unpack('<II', f.read(8))
        if cmd == 0x80000033:
            data = f.read(cmdsize - 8)
            dataoff, datasize = struct.unpack('<II', data[:8])
            print(f'LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS at file offset {off}: dataoff={dataoff} (0x{dataoff:x}) datasize={datasize}')
            # Read the fixups header
            f.seek(dataoff)
            fhdr = f.read(28)
            vals = struct.unpack('<IIIIIII', fhdr)
            print(f'  fixups_version={vals[0]} starts_offset={vals[1]} imports_offset={vals[2]}')
            print(f'  symbols_offset={vals[3]} imports_count={vals[4]} imports_format={vals[5]} symbols_format={vals[6]}')
        elif cmd == 0x80000034:
            data = f.read(cmdsize - 8)
            dataoff, datasize = struct.unpack('<II', data[:8])
            print(f'LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE at file offset {off}: dataoff={dataoff} (0x{dataoff:x}) datasize={datasize}')
        off += cmdsize
" 2>&1

import struct
with open('libFosterPlatform_x64.dylib', 'rb') as f:
    hdr = struct.unpack('<IIIIIIII', f.read(32))
    print(f'ncmds={hdr[4]} sizeofcmds={hdr[5]}')
    off = 32
    for i in range(hdr[4]):
        f.seek(off)
        cmd, cmdsize = struct.unpack('<II', f.read(8))
        if cmd == 0x80000033:
            dataoff, datasize = struct.unpack('<II', f.read(8))
            print(f'CHAINED_FIXUPS: dataoff=0x{dataoff:x} ({dataoff}) datasize={datasize}')
            f.seek(dataoff)
            vals = struct.unpack('<IIIIIII', f.read(28))
            print(f'  version={vals[0]} starts_off={vals[1]} imports_off={vals[2]} symbols_off={vals[3]} imports_count={vals[4]} imports_fmt={vals[5]} symbols_fmt={vals[6]}')
            # Check starts
            f.seek(dataoff + vals[1])
            seg_count = struct.unpack('<I', f.read(4))[0]
            print(f'  seg_count={seg_count}')
        elif cmd == 0x80000034:
            dataoff, datasize = struct.unpack('<II', f.read(8))
            print(f'EXPORTS_TRIE: dataoff=0x{dataoff:x} ({dataoff}) datasize={datasize}')
        off += cmdsize
" 2>&1

    # Check first bytes of exports trie

    # The original fat binary might have different offsets

    # and find the x86_64 slice offset
    with open('libFosterPlatform.dylib', 'rb') as f2:
        magic = struct.unpack('>I', f2.read(4))[0]
        print(f'Fat magic: 0x{magic:08x}')

        for i in range(narch):
            cpu, sub, foff, fsize, align = struct.unpack('>IIIII', f2.read(20))
            print(f'  arch {i}: cpu=0x{cpu:x} sub={sub} offset=0x{foff:x} size={fsize}')

Analyze fixups and first section offset
python3 -c "
import struct

with open('libFosterPlatform_x64.dylib', 'rb') as f:
    f.seek(0)
    hdr = struct.unpack('<IIIIIIII', f.read(32))
    print(f'Header: ncmds={hdr[4]} sizeofcmds={hdr[5]}')
    print(f'Load commands end at: {32 + hdr[5]}')
    
    # Find first section offset  
    off = 32
    for i in range(hdr[4]):
        f.seek(off)
        cmd, cmdsize = struct.unpack('<II', f.read(8))
        if cmd == 0x19:  # LC_SEGMENT_64
            segname = f.read(16).rstrip(b'\0').decode()
            vmaddr, vmsize, fileoff, filesize = struct.unpack('<QQQQ', f.read(32))
            maxprot, initprot, nsects, flags = struct.unpack('<IIII', f.read(16))
            print(f'  Segment {segname}: fileoff={fileoff} nsects={nsects}')
            for s in range(nsects):
                f.seek(off + 72 + s * 80)
                sectname = f.read(16).rstrip(b'\0').decode()
                segn = f.read(16).rstrip(b'\0').decode()
                addr, size, sect_off = struct.unpack('<QQI', f.read(20))
                if segname == '__TEXT' and s == 0:
                    print(f'    First section {sectname}: offset={sect_off} (0x{sect_off:x})')
        off += cmdsize
    
    # Now parse chained fixups to understand why only 17 fixups found
    f.seek(0x1d0000)
    vals = struct.unpack('<IIIIIII', f.read(28))
    print(f'\\nChained fixups: imports_count={vals[4]}')
    
    f.seek(0x1d0000 + vals[1])  # starts
    seg_count = struct.unpack('<I', f.read(4))[0]
    seg_offs = list(struct.unpack(f'<{seg_count}I', f.read(4*seg_count)))
    
    total_chains = 0
    for si in range(seg_count):
        if seg_offs[si] == 0:
            continue
        f.seek(0x1d0000 + vals[1] + seg_offs[si])
        sz, pgsz, pfmt = struct.unpack('<IHH', f.read(8))
        segoff = struct.unpack('<Q', f.read(8))[0]
        max_valid = struct.unpack('<I', f.read(4))[0]
        pgcount = struct.unpack('<H', f.read(2))[0]
        starts = list(struct.unpack(f'<{pgcount}H', f.read(2*pgcount)))
        non_none = sum(1 for s in starts if s != 0xFFFF)
        print(f'  Seg {si}: pages={pgcount}, non-empty={non_none}, ptr_fmt={pfmt}, segoff=0x{segoff:x}')
        total_chains += non_none
    
    print(f'Total chains: {total_chains}')
" 2>&1

Assistant2026-03-09T01:58:19.728Z




$ Bash


Trace chain walking with Python
python3 -c "
import struct

with open('libFosterPlatform_x64.dylib', 'rb') as f:
    # Parse segments
    f.seek(0)
    hdr = struct.unpack('<IIIIIIII', f.read(32))
    segs = []
    off = 32
    for i in range(hdr[4]):
        f.seek(off)
        cmd, cmdsize = struct.unpack('<II', f.read(8))
        if cmd == 0x19:
            segname = f.read(16).rstrip(b'\0').decode()
            vmaddr, vmsize, fileoff, filesize = struct.unpack('<QQQQ', f.read(32))
            segs.append((segname, vmaddr, vmsize, fileoff, filesize))
        off += cmdsize
    
    # Parse fixups
    f.seek(0x1d0000)
    fh = struct.unpack('<IIIIIII', f.read(28))
    
    # Read imports
    f.seek(0x1d0000 + fh[2])  # imports_offset
    imports = []
    for i in range(fh[4]):
        bits = struct.unpack('<I', f.read(4))[0]
        lib_ord = bits & 0xFF
        weak = (bits >> 8) & 1
        name_off = bits >> 9
        f2_pos = f.tell()
        f.seek(0x1d0000 + fh[3] + name_off)
        name = b''
        while True:
            c = f.read(1)
            if c == b'\0' or not c: break
            name += c
        imports.append((lib_ord, weak, name.decode('ascii', errors='replace')))
        f.seek(f2_pos)
    
    # Parse starts and walk chains
    f.seek(0x1d0000 + fh[1])
    seg_count = struct.unpack('<I', f.read(4))[0]
    seg_offs = list(struct.unpack(f'<{seg_count}I', f.read(4*seg_count)))
    
    total_r = 0; total_b = 0
    for si in range(seg_count):
        if seg_offs[si] == 0: continue
        f.seek(0x1d0000 + fh[1] + seg_offs[si])
        sz, pgsz, pfmt = struct.unpack('<IHH', f.read(8))
        segoff = struct.unpack('<Q', f.read(8))[0]
        max_valid = struct.unpack('<I', f.read(4))[0]
        pgcount = struct.unpack('<H', f.read(2))[0]
        starts = list(struct.unpack(f'<{pgcount}H', f.read(2*pgcount)))
        
        seg_fileoff = segs[si][3]
        print(f'Seg {si} ({segs[si][0]}): {pgcount} pages, fmt={pfmt}')
        
        for pg in range(pgcount):
            ps = starts[pg]
            if ps == 0xFFFF: continue
            
            off_in_seg = pg * pgsz + ps
            chain_len = 0
            binds_in_chain = 0
            
            while True:
                fpos = seg_fileoff + off_in_seg
                f.seek(fpos)
                raw = struct.unpack('<Q', f.read(8))[0]
                is_bind = (raw >> 63) & 1
                nxt = ((raw >> 44) & 0xFFF) * 4
                
                if is_bind:
                    ordinal = raw & 0xFFFFFF
                    if ordinal < len(imports):
                        name = imports[ordinal][2]
                        if chain_len < 3:  # only print first few
                            print(f'  pg{pg}+{chain_len}: BIND ord={ordinal} \"{name}\" next={nxt}')
                    total_b += 1
                    binds_in_chain += 1
                else:
                    total_r += 1
                
                chain_len += 1
                if nxt == 0: break
                off_in_seg += nxt
            
            if chain_len > 0 and pg < 3:
                print(f'  Page {pg}: {chain_len} entries ({binds_in_chain} binds)')
    
    print(f'\\nTotal: {total_r} rebases, {total_b} binds')
    print(f'Import table has {len(imports)} entries')
    print(f'First 5 imports: {[i[2] for i in imports[:5]]}')
" 2>&1

python3 -c "
import struct

with open('libFosterPlatform_x64.dylib', 'rb') as f:
    # Segment 1 (__DATA_CONST) fileoff
    # From earlier: segs[1] = __DATA_CONST, fileoff=1818624 (0x1bc000)
    # Page 0, start=? Let's get the actual page start
    f.seek(0x1d0000 + 32)  # starts_offset=32 -> seg_count at start
    seg_count = struct.unpack('<I', f.read(4))[0]
    seg_offs = list(struct.unpack(f'<{seg_count}I', f.read(4*seg_count)))
    
    # Seg 1 starts
    f.seek(0x1d0000 + 32 + seg_offs[1])
    sz, pgsz, pfmt = struct.unpack('<IHH', f.read(8))
    segoff = struct.unpack('<Q', f.read(8))[0]
    max_valid = struct.unpack('<I', f.read(4))[0]
    pgcount = struct.unpack('<H', f.read(2))[0]
    starts = list(struct.unpack(f'<{pgcount}H', f.read(2*pgcount)))
    
    print(f'Seg 1 page 0 start: {starts[0]} (0x{starts[0]:x})')
    
    # Read first few entries in the chain
    file_base = 0x1bc000  # __DATA_CONST fileoff
    off = starts[0]
    for i in range(20):
        f.seek(file_base + off)
        raw = struct.unpack('<Q', f.read(8))[0]
        is_bind = (raw >> 63) & 1
        
        # Try different bit positions for next
        next_44 = ((raw >> 44) & 0xFFF) * 4
        next_51 = ((raw >> 51) & 0xFFF) * 4
        
        if is_bind:
            ordinal = raw & 0xFFFFFF
            addend = (raw >> 24) & 0xFF
            print(f'  [{i}] off=0x{off:x}: BIND ord={ordinal} add={addend} raw=0x{raw:016x} next@44={next_44} next@51={next_51}')
        else:
            target = raw & 0xFFFFFFFFF  # 36 bits
            print(f'  [{i}] off=0x{off:x}: REBASE target=0x{target:x} raw=0x{raw:016x} next@44={next_44} next@51={next_51}')
        
        # Use next@51 to advance
        nxt = next_51
        if nxt == 0: 
            print(f'  Chain ends at entry {i}')
            break
        off += nxt
" 2>&1
